PAGE: Gamlen Amell
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Gamlen_Amell
======================================================================

Character
Gamlen Amell
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Location
Gamlen's House
,
Lowtown
The Blooming Rose
,
Hightown
Quests
The Destruction of Lothering
Birthright
All That Remains
Gamlen's Greatest Treasure
Family
Aristide Amell
(father)
Bethann Walker
(mother)
Charade Amell
(daughter)
Leandra Amell
(sister)
Hawke
(nephew/niece)
Bethany Hawke
(niece)
Carver Hawke
(nephew)
Fausten Amell
(uncle)
Damion Amell
(cousin)
Revka Amell
(cousin)
Human Magi
(cousin, once removed)
Voice
Timothy Watson
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Legacy
(mentioned)
Dragon Age: Inquisition
(mentioned)
Gamlen Amell
is the brother of
Leandra Amell
and uncle of
Hawke
,
Bethany
and
Carver
.
Background
Gamlen was the second child of Lord Aristide and Lady Bethann of House
Amell
, born a year after his sister
Leandra
. Like his sister, he was afforded the best tutoring and upbringing the Amells could buy. And though their parents favored his beautiful and talented sister, the two remained close throughout childhood onto maturity.
Gamlen acquired a taste for gambling as a young man, and what began as an innocent nobleman's pastime progressed to having to pawn off family heirlooms to pay off his debts. Lord Aristide cut Gamlen's allowance when he found out, and put Gamlen under house guard to prevent him from sneaking out at night. Gamlen tried to curb his gambling addiction, but sneaked out nonetheless whenever his pockets grew too heavy. Gamlen also used his skill at sneaking out of the house and seedy contacts to facilitate
Malcolm Hawke
and Leandra's courtship.
After Leandra eloped to Ferelden with Malcolm, Gamlen was left to care for their grief-stricken parents. Lady Bethann grew pale and thin, barely spoke to anyone or ate anything. She refused all invitations to soirees and balls. Lord Aristide began taking his meals in his office. The servants started going to Gamlen for instructions, who left the responsibilities of running the house to the steward. The oppressive atmosphere became too much for him, and he spent more time away from home, losing himself in drink, cards and the ladies of
the Blooming Rose
. Leandra sent him a letter when
Hawke
was born, but Gamlen was unable to write a reply that didn't sound accusatory and the letter went unanswered.
During this time, Gamlen befriended and eventually fell in love with
Mara Hartling
, one of the estate's chambermaids and daughter of the old head cook. When Lord Aristide and Lady Bethann were stricken with cholera, it was Gamlen and Mara who nursed them. They got better, though they never regained their full strength. Bethann died after a second bout in 9:10, while Lord Aristide clung to life until 9:11.
Mara stayed with Gamlen despite the numerous scandals the Amells were faced with. She found employment with the Reinhardts, a noble family once close to the Amells. When Gamlen kept gambling the nights away, Mara eventually left him, saying that she wouldn't let him waste another life like he'd wasted his.
Appearance
Gamlen's appearance varies with Hawke's facial preset and skintone
Gamlen has one of several facial structures and hair styles, depending on the customization of the player's character. The selection works as follows:
There are three base facial shapes that each family member can have. Hawkes using the default Hawke appearance or any of the first three presets will get the first head shape, Hawkes using the second three presets will get the second head shape, and Hawkes using the final three presets (or any modded presets past that) will get the third shape.
Each of the three head shapes has three variations - one with a pale skintone, one with a medium skintone, and one with a dark skintone, and each with a different hairstyle. Which of these variations is used by the game depends on Hawke's skintone; the first four skintones will result in the light-skinned version of Gamlen, the second four in the medium-skinned version, and the final four in the dark-skinned version. The same applies for
Carver
,
Bethany
and
Leandra
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
When Leandra and her children flee from
Lothering
during the
Fifth Blight
, they make their way to Kirkwall and seek Gamlen's aid in entering the city. However, he has gambled away the family fortune, and sold the
Amell estate
to
Tevinter
slavers. He now lives in
Lowtown
. When Hawke arrives to Kirkwall, the
Kirkwall City Guard
is denying access to all
Fereldan
refugees. In order to get his family in, Gamlen commits Hawke and their sibling to working with either a
mercenary company
or a
smuggling group
for a year. During which time the Hawke family live at
Gamlen's House
in Lowtown.
When Hawke breaks into the Amell family estate and brings back their grandfather's will, it is revealed that Leandra and her children were to inherit the estate, while Gamlen was to live on a stipend, controlled only by his sister.
By 9:34
Dragon
, following Hawke's successful expedition to the
Deep Roads
, Hawke had enough money to buy back the Amell estate.  While Leandra and her eldest child have relocated to their ancestral home in
Hightown
, Gamlen remains in his Lowtown hovel. He and Leandra have a standing weekly visit, however, when Leandra
vanishes
and fails to appear for their regular get-together, Gamlen goes to Hightown to alert Hawke to Leandra's disappearance. Hawke's later investigation reveals that Leandra was kidnapped by a
blood mage
serial killer,
Quentin
, taking women who resembled his deceased wife. Although Quentin is killed, Leandra perishes as well. Hawke can optionally inform Gamlen of Quentin's plan, the result of which is that Gamlen lashes out at Hawke for not rescuing Leandra in time. Whether he knows the details of Leandra's death or not, Gamlen then voluntarily shoulders the burden of breaking the news to
Bethany
or
Carver
, noting that Hawke has enough on their mind.
By 9:37 Dragon, Hawke bears the title of
Champion of Kirkwall
. Gamlen himself remarks that he thought that the Amell line would die with him and is glad that Hawke pulled it out of the grave.
Hawke
discovers
a note referencing the
Gem of Keroshek
, a rare jewel which Gamlen had wasted a good portion of his life and family fortune trying to find. When Hawke follows the odd series of clues to their ultimate conclusion, Hawke discovers that Gamlen has a daughter,
Charade
, of whose existence he is completely unaware. Charade arranged the whole thing to see how far Gamlen would go to recover the jewel. Hawke may take the jewel for him/herself, or encourage Charade to meet her father and develop a relationship. If the latter occurs, Gamlen is pleased with his daughter and grateful to Hawke, remarking that
Malcolm Hawke
must have been a decent individual if he raised a child like Hawke, though he also reiterates his demand that Hawke refrain from meddling in his affairs from now on.
Legacy
If Bethany/Carver did not survive the Deep Roads Expedition, Gamlen speaks to Hawke regarding Malcolm's actions. He then recounts how Malcolm and Leandra met, and how he distracted their father, Aristide Amell, to allow the two to talk.

Trivia
During a conversation with Anders in his
Questioning Beliefs (Anders Act 2)
, a Humorous Hawke may jokingly question "Why do none of my friends ever just want to be the best Wallop player in Lowtown?" Later, during the Act 3 quest
Gamlen's Greatest Treasure
, it is revealed that Gamlen keeps his old Wallop Mallet on the wall in his house, and he explains that he used to play as a boy. He also asserts that playing Wallop was the "Last time I was any good at anything." This may indicate that Gamlen himself is actually the best Wallop player in Lowtown.
In
Dragon Age: Inquisition
, Hawke may mention that Gamlen is still in Kirkwall.
The
Dwarven Merchants' Guild
loaned Gamlen a significant amount of money for a business venture involving the import of an
Ander
delicacy, which however failed. As he was unable to pay back the money, the Merchants' Guild sent the
Carta
to Hawke in order to collect from them sometime between 9:34 and 9:37 Dragon. But in a surprising turn of events Carta's debt collectors were dissuaded by Hawke and did not further pursue the matter.

Character
Gascard DuPuis
Title
Minor Noble
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Class
Mage
Specialization
Blood Mage
Rank
Lieutenant
Location
Hightown
,
Kirkwall
Lowtown
,
Kirkwall
Quests
Prime Suspect
All That Remains
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Gascard DuPuis
is an
Orlesian
noble
who now lives in
Kirkwall
. He is a reclusive man who rarely leaves his estate in
Hightown
.
Knight-Templar
Emeric
suspects him of being involved in a series of gruesome murders.
Background
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Gascard successfully hid his magic all his life. He was eventually chosen to be
Quentin
's apprentice. Gascard admired Quentin for daring to push the boundaries of what was possible. However, their relationship soured after the death of Quentin's wife left him distraught. Quentin became reclusive, refusing to include Gascard in his work. Eventually, Gascard broke into Quentin's study to see what his master was working on, and was greatly impressed by Quentin's feat of necromancy. When Quentin discovered the break-in, he sent Gascard away and disappeared with his research.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Gascard is involved in the quest
Prime Suspect
. Emeric suspects Gascard of being linked to the serial killer that has been operating in Kirkwall for the past three years and asks that
Hawke
investigates, as
Knight-Commander
Meredith
has forbidden him from pursuing the investigation himself after a search of the DuPuis estate turned up nothing.
When Hawke goes to search the DuPuis estate, they are attacked by shades, giving credibility to Emeric's suspicions. Finding evidence that Gascard is a
blood mage
and is searching for mages escaped from the Starkhaven Circle, Hawke eventually finds Gascard with a woman named
Alessa
. Gascard claims to be innocent of the murders. He says that he is in fact hunting the true killer, who murdered his sister several years ago, and that he only took Alessa to protect her, as she was to be the killer's next victim. When Alessa says that Gascard hurt her, he explains that he only took her blood so he could track her with blood magic should she be abducted. She doesn't believe him and runs out of the estate, fleeing for her life. Gascard is concerned that she will link him to the murders.
Hawke can either kill him or offer their assistance in finding the killer. If Hawke tries to kill him, Gascard flees to several rooms in the manor, summoning shades and
demons
to fight for him, before being tracked down and killed. Otherwise, he refuses Hawke's help and leaves, telling Hawke he is going to
Darktown
. Letting him go while Aveline or Isabela is in the party results in:
Aveline: rivalry (
+5
)
Isabela: rivalry (
+5
)
After Emeric's death at the hands of a shade, Hawke can tell
the templar
who arrives to investigate where Gascard is, leading to his arrest and execution for the murders.
If Hawke did not tell the templars where Gascard is he can be found in Darktown after
Leandra
is kidnapped. By performing a blood magic ritual, he can locate Alessa and take Hawke to her. Bringing Hawke to Quentin's lair, Gascard confronts Quentin, revealing that he lied when he said his sister had been murdered. In truth, Quentin was Gascard's former mentor. When Quentin, who had gone insane from the loss of his wife, refused to share the secrets of necromancy with his apprentice, Gascard spent years tracking him down to learn his magic.
Quentin offers to share his secrets with Gascard if he helps kill Hawke. Through the right dialogue choices, Gascard can be convinced to go against Quentin, but if he is not dissuaded he turns on the party. If Varric is in the party, he shoots Gascard through the throat before Hawke can do anything, looking at Hawke and saying "What? You were going to do that, right?"
If not killed during
Prime Suspect
or
All That Remains
, Gascard can later be found in Darktown, in the same location where he was to perform the blood ritual. If Aveline or Fenris is in the group, they can be called on to make Gascard talk. Fenris will force Gascard to reveal that he knew it was Quentin from the start, while Aveline will convince Quentin to confess that he would not have told Hawke if he knew Leandra was an intended victim. Gascard will also acknowledge that he never had a sister and the portrait in his house is of a woman he experimented on to learn more about necromancy. He can then either be executed, resulting in:
Isabela: friendship (
+10
)
Or he can be allowed to leave, resulting in:
Isabela: rivalry (
+10
)
If allowed to leave, he sends you a
letter
and package at the beginning of Act 3, stating that he has given up magic.
Quests
Prime Suspect
All That Remains
(conditional)
Note texts
A Package from Gascard DuPuis
(conditional)
Bugs
pc

All That Remains
.
pc

pc

White Scapular of the Defender
should be included with the Act 3 letter, but is not.

PAGE: Gerav
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters

Character
Gerav
Race
Dwarf
(
Ghoul
)
Gender
Male
Class
Rogue
Rank
Lieutenant
Caste
No caste
(
surfacer
)
Affiliation
Carta
Corypheus
Location
Carta Hideout
Quests
Legacy
Appearances
Dragon Age II
-
Legacy
Gerav
is a
surface dwarf
and member of the
Carta
and also an acquaintance of
Varric
.
Background
While working for the Carta Gerav had an idea of constructing a repeating crossbow that was easy to operate and aim. His bosses saw the opportunity in such a revolutionary weapon and funded his research. He made the first prototype in the first week but it didn't work and neither the numerous more prototypes he made. His bosses were getting restless when Varric Tethras learned about Gerav's work and purchased his Number Fourteen prototype which was the closest to work before the designs started becoming more and more extreme. Unbeknown to Gerav and the Carta, Varric gave his crossbow to
Bianca Davri
who was a young smith at the time and she managed to redesign
the crossbow and fix its deficiencies. When the Carta learned that Varric's
repeating crossbow
was working he told Gerav that he simply adjusted some of her pins.
So Gerav's bosses gave him even more gold in an effort to replicate the success of Number Fourteen prototype. When Gerav had time he also built small upgrades for the crossbow, which was now called Bianca. However some years later he disappeared when he drank
darkspawn
blood and became one of the thralls of
Corypheus
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
In 9:37
Dragon
Gerav is tasked with capturing
Hawke
. He is encountered in the Carta fortress and, like the rest of the
dwarves
there, Gerav is insane and has been corrupted by the
darkspawn
taint. If Varric is in the party the two will recognize each other with Gerav being reluctant to fight his old friend instead saying that he only wants Hawke. Varric will attempt to make Gerav see reason. He also reveals to Hawke that Gerav is a brilliant dwarf and that his current behavior is not typical of him. However Varric fails to convince Gerav so he decides to put him out of his misery. Gerav manages to avoid the crossbow's shot and summons allies, much to Varric's dismay and anger. Once defeated, Varric is regretful of what he had to do and reveals that Gerav made his crossbow.
Gerav fights like any other Carta assassin, he will attempt to flank the player and backstab them, he will also be joined by other Carta members, including a couple of
assassins
. He will drop
Turquoise Ring of the Archon
that only Varric can wear. If Varric is not in the party, Gerav will still appear and another party member will comment on Gerav's insanity, but his involvement with Varric's past is not revealed and he will attack Hawke on sight along with some Carta members. Upon death he will drop the same loot as well as an item named
A Letter to Gerav
.
Quests
Legacy
Quotes
"The Hawke's blood! The Master will rise. He will be free!"
"The Master must be free..."
"We drink the darkspawn blood. He calls us..."
"It's the only way... to hear the music."
Codex entries
A Letter to Gerav
Notes
On
Nightmare difficulty
, he is completely immune to elemental damage. You can only hit him with physical damage.

Dragon Age II
Ghyslain de Carrac
is an Orlesian living in
Kirkwall
. He is married to Ninette, though their marriage is in turmoil.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Ghyslain de Carrac is involved in the quest
the First Sacrifice
. After his wife goes missing, he puts up
a reward
for her safe return. When
Hawke
talks to him, he explains that his marriage is failing and that he wants his wife to be found so that her family, who is suspecting him of having done something to her, will not ruin him. He denies hurting Ninette and points Hawke towards the men that she was cheating with, such as
Jethann
at the
Blooming Rose
.
When Hawke's investigation uncovers human remains in a
Lowtown
foundry, Ghyslain identifies Ninette's wedding ring, which reads "Forever faithful, forever yours." He expresses some regret for the way his marriage has turned out, but mostly relief that Ninette's family cannot ruin him and rewards Hawke. If Hawke chooses to tell him the exact circumstances of how the ring was found, Ghyslain will return the ring, not wanting to leave any possibility of being linked to her death and blamed by her family.

Dragon Age II
Ginnis
is the cold-hearted leader of a mercenary group known as
the Winters
.
Background
The Winters originate from
Nevarra
. Ginnis travels to the
Free Marches
looking to establish a foothold in
Kirkwall
. She has a notorious reputation of always getting the job done.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Ginnis is involved in the quest
the Unbidden Rescue
. She first encounters
Hawke
at the
Viscount's Keep
to inquire about a reward for the rescue of the
Viscount
's son,
Saemus Dumar
. After accepting the mission from Seneschal
Bran
, Ginnis tracks the Viscount's son to the
Wounded Coast
where she discovers him traveling with a lone Qunari. Ginnis mercilessly butchers Saemus'
Qunari
companion, Ashaad. In response, Saemus becomes furious at Ginnis, using Qunari
words
to insult her. Suspecting that Saemus has converted, Ginnis threatens to cut the boy's tongue out before spotting
Hawke
. When Saemus offers to let Hawke claim the bounty for returning him, Ginnis becomes hostile and attacks Hawke alongside several Winters soldiers. They are killed in the conflict.

Character
Guillaume de Launcet
Title

Race

,

Quests

Family

(father)

(wife)

(son)
Fifi de Launcet
(daughter)
Babette de Launcet
(daughter)
More unnamed children
Voice
Jamie Glover
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Dragon Age: Inquisition
(mentioned)
Comte
Guillaume de Launcet
is a
minor noble
from
Orlais
. For whatever reasons, he and
his wife
live in
Kirkwall
.
Background
Guillaume de Launcet was the eldest son of Comte Reynaud de Launcet, a minor Orlesian noble. As a child, Guillaume was betrothed to
Leandra Amell
.
The next summer Guillaume met Leandra for the first time at his father's country estate.
Several years after their betrothal, Leandra fell in love with
Malcolm Hawke
, a
mage
, and fell pregnant with his
child
. She briefly considered marrying Guillaume and passing the baby off as his. When Leandra went to break off her relationship with Malcolm, he used the opportunity to propose. Leandra accepted Malcolm's proposal and left for
Ferelden
with him.
Sometime after Leandra broke off their engagement, Guillaume met and married a woman named Dulci with whom he had several children. One of their children,
Emile
was discovered to be a mage at the age of six, and was taken to the Kirkwall
Circle of Magi
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Guillaume is involved in the quest
On The Loose
.
After Knight-Commander
Meredith
asks
Hawke
to retrieve three magi who have escaped the Circle, Hawke goes to the de Launcet manor in
Hightown
. There, while Hawke talks to Dulci about Emile, Guillaume bursts into the room and begins to rant about how much trouble his son is causing. Dulci then reveals that she gave Emile some money to leave Kirkwall and begin a new life. Hawke must then go to
The Hanged Man
and talk to Emile. Emile can be turned in to the
Templars
or allowed to leave in order to start his new life outside of Kirkwall. If Emile is allowed to leave, Dulci sends Hawke a thank you letter along with some gold. If Emile returns to the Circle and is allowed to sleep with a tavern girl named Nella, Meredith will claim that she wanted to have Emile executed immediately, but that Guillaume made an impassioned plea in his defense and depending upon Hawke's response, Meredith will also claim that Guillaume implied that Emile was an idiot. Nella will then come to the de Launcet manor, claiming to be pregnant with his child; Guillaume comments that he should hide her on the country estate. Guillaume will also send Hawke a thank you letter along with some gold in this instance.
Quests
On the Loose
Note texts
A Message from the Comte de Launcet
Trivia
Some de Launcets might be attending the
peace talks
in
Halamshiral
. A noble can be heard saying "Are all the de Launcets here?" while another replies "Maker, I hope not!"

Character
Hadriana
Title

Race

Appearances
Dragon Age II
Hadriana
is a
Tevinter
Magister
and the apprentice of
Danarius
.
Background
Hadriana is described as a social climber who was cruel to her master's
slaves
, depriving them of food and sleep.
Fenris
claims she would sell her own children in order to please her master. She was mocked and laughed at by other magisters; this ridicule led to her cruelty, steadily tearing away the decency within her.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Hadriana is involved in Fenris' companion quest
A Bitter Pill
. Danarius sent her to
Kirkwall
to re-capture his escaped slave, Fenris. Hadriana sends another mage and several soldiers to apprehend Fenris while he and
Hawke
cross the
Wounded Coast
. However, the ambush fails and Fenris and Hawke learn of Hadriana's arrival. With Fenris and Hawke in pursuit, Hadriana prepares to face Fenris at the
Holding Caves
outside
Kirkwall
, securing the slave pens with soldiers and sacrificing
Orana
's father to enhance her magic for the coming confrontation with Fenris.
Once defeated, Hadriana offers Fenris information about his past if he agrees to spare her, and reveals that he still has a living relative; his sister,
Varania
. Fenris agrees, but slays her anyway after she has given him the information he needs.
Quests
A Bitter Pill
Bugs
In combat, if
Petrify
followed by
Gravitic Ring
is cast with her in the middle, she will no longer attack and can no longer be killed.

Harley Casimi
is a lieutenant in the
Kirkwall City Guard
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Harley can be encountered on the
Wounded Coast
. She and her fellow guards are under attack by several members of
Evets
' Marauders, an infamous band of raiders. Though they are taking casualties, Harley refuses to retreat, as it would allow the raiders to escape and continue terrorizing the coast. She asks
Hawke
for help in taking them down. If
Aveline
is present, she tells Hawke that Harley is one of her guards, and that she was recently promoted. Harley mentions that this is her first patrol. Hawke can convince the guards to join them in the fight against
Fell Orden
and the other raiders, tell them to wait while they clear the area, or simply walk away from the fight.
If
Fell Orden
is defeated, Harley thanks Hawke and tells then to see
Jalen
for a reward. She then calls her remaining guards and leads them back towards Kirkwall.

Trivia

PAGE: Hubert Bartiere
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Hubert_Bartiere
======================================================================

Character
Hubert Bartiere
Title
Businessman
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Location
Hightown
,
Kirkwall
Quests
The Bone Pit
Get Back to Work
Inside Job
Mine Massacre
Voice
Stephane Cornicard
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Hubert
is a merchant working in
Kirkwall
and the foreman of
the Bone Pit
mining site. He sells items at
Hubert's Fine Goods
in
Hightown
.
Background
Hubert appears to be from
Orlais
. Not much else is known about his past other than he has claimed to have sold a seat cushion to Empress
Celene
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Hubert is involved in the quest
the Bone Pit
. A letter arrives at
Hawke
's home from
Meeran
or
Athenril
and directs them to speak to a merchant named Hubert. Upon speaking to Hubert, he will send Hawke to go and clear out the
Bone Pit
mining site. Hawke arrives only to find the place infested with
dragonlings
and
dragons
. After clearing out the mine and killing a
mature dragon
, Hawke must return to Hubert and tell him the news. When Hubert hears that it was dragons that Hawke had to deal with, he offers Hawke a 50/50 ownership of the Bone Pit and asks that Hawke protects it in the future.
Accepting Hubert's deal will trigger the quest
Get Back to Work
.
In 9:34 Dragon, Hubert deduces that the mining operation has been the victim of an
Inside Job
. After some of his cargo is stolen, Hubert discovers that an employee named
Sabin
has betrayed him and asks Hawke to interrogate him as he claims to be from Hawke's
home village
. Sabin claims that he was only looking out for his family and that he is sorry. Hubert enlists the help of a
Coterie
member,
Lilley
. From there, Hawke can decide what to do with Sabin, either convincing Hubert to free him, allowing Lilley to kill him (which Hubert wishes for), or sending him to jail. After dealing with Sabin, Hawke must then go to
Darktown
and meet up with
Lilley
. Unfortunately, Hawke finds her dead and must go on to kill another Coterie member,
Brekker
, who is responsible for stealing Hubert's cargo.
Finally in 9:37 Dragon, Hubert once again asks Hawke to investigate the Bone Pit after a caravan was completely destroyed, with all killed save for a single horse. Hawke's investigation into the
Mine Massacre
, leads Hawke to discover that a
high dragon
has made a nest in the Bone Pit, and drives it out. Once Hubert is notified, Hubert will say that he is ruined, caring only for his lost equipment. He will then inform Hawke that he is focusing on his mercantile ventures. Hawke has the option to ask Hubert to give them complete ownership of the mine as payment so that they may rebuild it someday.
Quests
The Bone Pit
Get Back to Work
Inside Job
Mine Massacre
Note texts
The Bone Pit
Inside Job
Trivia
In
cut content
from
Dragon Age II
there is audio for an alternate version of Hubert's final quest in which he knew about the likelihood of an attack on the Bone Pit but neglected to evacuate the miners.
Some prostitutes at the
Blooming Rose
will discuss Hubert's requests to rub his feet, and the stench of his feet that makes them refuse his request.

Background
Hugh is one of many templar recruits being trained in
the Gallows
in 9:31
Dragon
, along with
Keran
,
Paxley
,
Ruvena
and

.
Involvement
Hugh is in involved in the quest

. Hugh later runs afoul of his fellow Templars and finds himself a pariah for publicly speaking out against Knight-Commander

Three years later, Hugh,
Paxley
,

Carver
in the

demo.

Character
Hugin
Title

Race
Dwarf
Gender
Male
Caste
No caste
(
surfacer
)
Location

,
Hightown
Quests
Family Matter
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Hugin
is a
surface dwarf
who works as
Bartrand Tethras
' steward in
Kirkwall
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Hugin is involved in the quest
Family Matter
. After
Hawke
enters
Bartrand's Estate
with
Varric Tethras
, Varric meets up with Hugin, who then tells him that after Bartrand left Varric and Hawke to die in the
Primeval Thaig
, he started hearing voices, claiming the
lyrium Idol
taken from the
thaig
was talking and singing to him. At the same time, he was scared by it and sold it during one of his "better days". Unfortunately, he could still hear the relic and was eventually driven mad by it.
The steward tells Varric and Hawke that Bartrand started feeding the servants and guards
lyrium
to make them hear the "song" and became increasingly mad as no results materialized, to the point that he started torturing the servants and cutting bits off them while still alive. Hugin begs Varric and Hawke to give anything alive in Bartrand's study a quick and merciful death before fleeing.
Quests
Family Matter

PAGE: Huon

======================================================================

“I am a visionary. I've seen our destiny. I know what fate holds for the elves.”
Character
Huon
Title
Mage
(formerly)
Race
Elf
Gender
Male
Class
Mage
Specialization
Blood Mage
Affiliation
Circle of Magi
(formerly)
Location
Kirkwall Alienage
,
Lowtown
(night)
Quests
On the Loose
Family
Nyssa
(wife)
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Huon
is an elven
mage
of the
Kirkwall
Circle of Magi
.
Background
Huon lived in the
Kirkwall Alienage
for a number of years with his wife,
Nyssa
. He was said to be a nice and caring husband. Unfortunately, the
templars
found out that he was an
apostate
mage. They chained him and dragged him away in front of all his neighbors. For ten years, Huon lived in the
Kirkwall Circle
of Magi until he and a number of other magi destroyed their
phylacteries
and escaped. Huon was one of only three who managed to evade capture.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Huon is involved in the quest
On The Loose
. After
Knight-Commander
Meredith
asks
Hawke
to retrieve three mages that have escaped the Circle, Hawke follows Huon's trail to the alienage. There, Hawke finds Nyssa, who tells Hawke that after the templars left, Huon returned and asked her to hide him. Nyssa was scared and told him to leave. He did as she asked, but she fears he may return. At night, Hawke returns to the alienage just as Huon stabs Nyssa, planning to use her blood to show the world "true elven power" using blood magic. Huon sees Hawke and summons
shades
and
demons
, forcing Hawke to kill him.
Quests
On the Loose
Notable loot
Formula: Fell Poison
Boots of the Champion
(class specific)
Trivia
Huon has a tattoo of the
dwarven
character for "C" - the brand of a casteless.
Bugs
There is a glitch when Huon does not show up after dying, preventing you from being able to loot his body.
Huon will sometimes drop the Boots of the Champion for all three classes instead of only your current class.

confirmation needed
]

PAGE: Idunna
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Idunna
======================================================================

Character
Idunna
Race
Human
Gender
Female
Class
Mage
Specialization
Blood Mage
Location
The Blooming Rose
Quests
Enemies Among Us
Forbidden Knowledge
Voice
Kellie Bright
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Idunna
is a sex worker in
Kirkwall
's brothel,
the Blooming Rose
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Idunna is involved in the quest
Enemies Among Us
. Several
templar recruits
have recently gone missing. Tasked with finding the cause,
Hawke
finds that the missing templars frequented the Blooming Rose.
Viveka
, a book keeper at the brothel, informs Hawke that the templars in question were customers of Idunna. When Hawke finds Idunna, she uses
blood magic
to force Hawke to reveal the source of their information and attempts to make Hawke slit their own throat. However, Hawke manages to overcome the spell. At this point, Hawke can either kill her or spare her and hand her over to the templars. Regardless of choice, Hawke finds that she was linked to a plot to have templar recruits forcibly possessed by demons then returned to the order to sow chaos in their ranks.
If Idunna is spared, she sends Hawke a
letter
revealing she's repented and is now following the
Maker
. She wants evil tomes teaching blood magic destroyed, but can't do it herself because the templars will not permit her to leave her cell.
If Hawke has a
mage
companion
in the party when talking to her, they have the option of asking them to interrupt Idunna's spell. Doing this later gives you a
(
+5
) with that character. If Hawke is a mage, then they may simply break Idunna's control themselves. However, there are no friendship or rivalry points rewarded for doing so.
Killing her results in:
Isabela: friendship (
+5
)
Carver: friendship (
+5
)
Sparing her and sending her to the templars:
Isabela: rivalry (
+5
)
Anders: rivalry (
+5
)
Quests
Act 1
Enemies Among Us
Act 2
Forbidden Knowledge
(conditional)
Note texts
Forbidden Knowledge

PAGE: Iwan
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Iwan
======================================================================

“We were after a
dwarven
weapon, trying to make sure it stayed in dwarven hands!”
Character
Iwan
Title
Merchant
Race
Dwarf
Gender
Male
Caste
No caste
(
surfacer
)
Location
Hightown
,
Kirkwall
(conditional)
Deep Roads
(conditional)
Quests
Fool's Gold
Family
Yevhen
(father)
Merin
(brother)
Emrys
(brother)
Voice
Jason Singer
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Iwan
is a
surface dwarf
who, wishing to follow in
Hawke
's footsteps, ventured into the
Deep Roads
with his brothers in search for treasure.
Background
Iwan is
Yevhen
's middle son and works as a merchant. The boldest of the three brothers, he is also the most unscrupulous. He and his brothers were raised by an
elven
woman named
Dera
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Note:
Iwan will only be encountered if a
Dragon Age: Origins
save where
Nathaniel Howe
died or was never recruited into the
Grey Wardens
was imported.
Iwan is involved in the quest
Fool's Gold
. Yevhen, who has ties with the
Dwarven Merchants' Guild
, desperately asks
Hawke
to retrieve his three sons who have gone down into the
Deep Roads
, by themselves, in search of treasure. Once down there, Hawke finds Yevhen's oldest son,
Emrys
, sitting in front of a locked door. He explains that his younger brother, Iwan, locked the youngest brother,
Merin
, in a room full of
darkspawn
before scampering off to find the treasure. Hawke then tells Emrys to go back to his father and must now choose which brother to save. If Hawke goes around the locked door and goes to the room Merin is locked in, Hawke and company must help him fight off a small troop of darkspawn. This act will save Merin who will then go back to his father. However, doing this will result in Iwan's death.
Alternatively, Hawke can bypass Merin's tomb and run straight to Iwan. Helping Iwan fight off his darkspawn will result in Merin's death. Hawke can then lie to Yevhen or tell him what Iwan really did, in which case Iwan is cast out of his
family
.
Quests
Fool's Gold
(conditional)
Gallery
The quest choices in
Dragon Age Keep

PAGE: Jalen
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Jalen
======================================================================

“Thanks again for your help.”
Character
Jalen
Title
Lieutenant
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Affiliation
Kirkwall City Guard
Location
Viscount's Keep
Quests
Raiders on the Cliffs
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Jalen
is a lieutenant in the
Kirkwall City Guard
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
After
Hawke
helps Lieutenant
Harley Casimi
with
raiders
on the
Wounded Coast
, she tells them to speak to Jalen in the
Viscount's Keep
for a reward. In the Keep, Jalen asks Hawke if they killed all the raiders. Hawke mentions killing
Fell Orden
, but Jalen notes that the leader of the raiders,
Evets
, wasn't among the casualties. He tells Hawke to be careful, as Evets will most likely want revenge on Hawke for killing his men. Then Jalen thanks Hawke for helping Harley and rewards them.
Quests
Raiders on the Cliffs
Trivia
Jalen warns Hawke about Evets and mentions there is a large bounty on his head. Evets himself confronts Hawke three years later at the eastern entrance to the Wounded Coast, seeking vengeance for his fallen comrades—but is killed by Hawke in the process.

PAGE: Jan
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Jan
======================================================================

“Give it away. You have to give it away, and not get it back. That's the term of the curse.”
Character
Jan
Race
Elf
Gender
Female
Rank
Rogue
Affiliation
Isabela
Location
The Dungeons
,
Chateau Haine
Quests
Pirates and their Curses
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Mark of the Assassin
Dragon Age: Inquisition
Jan
, also known as
Knife-Eared Jan
, is a pirate.
Background
Jan was a pirate who served on a ship called The Wicked Dancer under Captain Maldine. Maldine was a
maleficar
and cursed several members of her crew by turning them into stone after they stole from her. The only person who can break the curse is another pirate captain.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
If
Isabela
is brought along to
Chateau Haine
, she recognizes the trapped pirates and is able to talk to them. Jan reveals that her former captain , whom she calls a lying, cheating, scurvy bastard, placed a curse on them and asks that Isabela, as another pirate captain, break it. To do so, she tells her to find the
Dagger of the Four Winds
. When returned with the dagger, Jan reveals that Isabela has to give up the dagger in order to break the curse and free them. Hawke can choose to let Isabela keep the dagger, or have her free the pirates, in which case they pledge themselves to Isabela's service.
Jan,
Paisley Pete
and Left-Hand
Rawley
will aid Hawke in the fight against
Cahir
in the cave if freed.
Quests
Pirates and their Curses
Trivia
The same statue can be found inside Daerwin's Mouth on the
Storm Coast
in
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Miniature versions of the statue can also be found atop a ruin in the
Western Approach
.
Gallery

======================================================================
PAGE: Jansen
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Jansen
======================================================================

Character
Jansen
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Location
The Bone Pit
Lowtown
,
Kirkwall
Quests
The Bone Pit
Get Back to Work
Cave Crawling
Cavern of Dead
Pick Up Pickaxes
Voice
Robin Atkin Downes
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Jansen
is a
Fereldan
miner working in
the Bone Pit
quarry outside of
Kirkwall
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
In Act 1, Jansen is involved in the quest
the Bone Pit
. After clearing out the mine, Hawke will stumble upon a survivor, Jansen, who warns that there is a large dragon further in the mine. After slaying the dragon, Hubert asks Hawke to find his surviving workers. During the quest
Get Back to Work
, Hawke has to convince them to return to the mine. The miners can be found in
Lowtown
, behind
the Hanged Man
.
Jansen and fellow miners during
Get Back to Work
In Act 2, Jansen is at the Bone Pit. He alerts Hawke to continual problems in the mine: an
infestation of spiders
, the
rise of undead
, and
subpar equipment
.
Once all these issues have been resolved, Jansen can be heard complaining about the smell in the lower mines and noting the sudden lack of animals in the surrounding areas and the disappearances of two of his friends (one of which was found "half eaten and with big claw marks.") After this he will only say "I always feel safer with you here boss". These plus the growling noises that can be heard in the background point to the
high dragon
that emerges in Act 3.
In Act 3, Hubert once again asks Hawke to investigate the Bone Pit after a caravan was completely destroyed, with no survivors save a horse. During the quest
Mine Massacre
, Hawke discovers that a high dragon has made a nest in the Bone Pit and slays it; it is presumed Jansen was killed when the dragon emerged.
Quests
Act 1
The Bone Pit
Get Back to Work
Act 2
Cave Crawling
Cavern of Dead
Pick Up Pickaxes

======================================================================
PAGE: Javaris Tintop
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Javaris_Tintop
======================================================================

“What a mess of mud and blood. No resale value at all.”
Character
Javaris Tintop
Title
Merchant
Race
Dwarf
Gender
Male
Caste
No caste
(
surfacer
)
Location
Docks
,
Kirkwall
Outside
Smuggler's Cut
,
Wounded Coast
Quests
Blackpowder Promise
Blackpowder Courtesy
Voice
Jason Singer
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Javaris Tintop
is a
surface dwarf
based out of
Kirkwall
and works as a merchant and investor. With the
Qunari
having recently come to Kirkwall, Javaris has been trying to get the Qunari to sell the recipe for an explosive black powder, known as gaatlok, to him.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Act 1
Varric mentions a rumor that Javaris is looking for
hired help
. Javaris is encountered for the first time at
Dead Man's Pass
when Hawke rescues him and his mercenary guards from an attack. Impressed by the skill of Hawke and their companions in combat, Javaris asks Hawke to kill
Tal-Vashoth
outlaws in an effort to appeal to the
Arishok
, who has refused all previous attempts at barter. Once Hawke destroys the Tal-Vashoth band, Javaris rendezvouses with Hawke at the
Qunari Compound
at the
Docks
. However Javaris is unable to persuade the Arishok to sell the formula and the Arishok is more impressed with Hawke than Javaris.
Act 2
The fate of Javaris Tintop in
Dragon Age Keep
Hawke encounters Javaris again in 9:34
Dragon
. The Arishok
tasks
Hawke to track down a Qunari poison, saar-qamek, which he believes Javaris stole, assuming it to be the formula for the gaatlok. Hawke learns from a Coterie barker selling Javaris' assets that the
dwarf
has made a run for it, leaving his debts behind as well. She trades Hawke Javaris' likely escape route,
Smuggler's Cut
, in lieu of repayment. Hawke eventually tracks Javaris down and Javaris claims he has been framed by an
elven
fanatic, who stole the saar-qamek and blamed Javaris for the theft. With the elf planning on killing him and the Qunari presuming him to be a thief, Javaris had decided to make a run for it. Hawke can either accept Javaris' explanation or execute him.
Quests
Act 1
Blackpowder Promise
Act 2
Blackpowder Courtesy
Trivia
If Hawke accepts Javaris' explanation and lets him free, the dwarf will start looting the body of a dead bodyguard. At that moment you can click him to hear several comical lines, the last one breaking the fourth wall.

Dragon Age II
Jethann
is a prostitute in
The Blooming Rose
.
Involvement
He is encountered during the quest
the First Sacrifice
. He was seeing Ninette de Carrac and is saddened to learn of her death.
After this first conversation,
Hawke
can sleep with him, regardless of the player's gender. If Hawke sleeps with him and
Carver
/
Bethany
or
Aveline
is in the party, then Carver / Bethany
(
+5
) and Aveline
(
+5
).
While his quest is active, it seems Hawke cannot interact with Madame Lusine to partner with any other prostitute on the premises. The only way to end this is if Hawke sleeps with Jethann or tells him about Ninette's death.
Quests
The First Sacrifice
Trivia
Isabela
says that she likes Jethann because he reminds her of "someone I know".
Fenris
' sarcastic reply suggests he thinks it's herself.
Merrill
just outright states the fact, Isabela agrees.

is the Captain of the
city guard
of
Kirkwall
in 9:31
Dragon
.
Background
Jeven apparently replaced
Ewald
as Captain of the Guard sometime while the
Hawke
siblings
were in indentured servitude.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Jeven's arrest
Jeven is first encountered during
Aveline
's first
companion quest
,
the Way It Should Be
.
Jeven flies into a rage when Aveline informs him that she and Hawke cleared a route infested with bandits, threatening to have them jailed if a similar incident occurs. When Aveline investigates this further, it transpires that Jeven has become indebted to the infamous
Coterie
. In an attempt to repay them, he sends guards on patrol with "a satchel" containing valuable information. The premise of this scheme was to sacrifice the guardsman and allow the Coterie to reap the reward. Jeven is arrested by his own guardsmen, and replaced by Aveline as Captain.
Note:
If
the Way It Should Be
was not completed, Aveline will automatically assume the position of Captain in Act 2, and
Favor and Fault
will not occur during Act 3.
Jeven later returns to Kirkwall and is encountered during Aveline's companion quest
Favor and Fault
.
Jeven rallying anti-Ferelden militia
Since his fall from grace, Jeven has taken up with base types who hold prejudiced views against
Fereldans
like Aveline and Hawke. He becomes the leader of a dangerous group of insurgents who are prejudiced against any Fereldans in a position of authority in the city. Jeven attempts to have Captain Aveline expelled by forging anonymous complaints that she was coddling her men. Jeven even attempts to coax guards into joining his cause but they refuse their disgraced former captain's offer. After disproving his false complaints, Aveline and Hawke subsequently track Jeven down while he is trying to rally more Kirkwallers to his cause in
Darktown
and is slain in the ensuing confrontation.
Quests
Act 1
The Way It Should Be
Act 3
Favor and Fault
(conditional)

Character
Johane Harimann
Title
Lady
Race
Human

Female

Mage
Specialization
Blood Mage
Rank
Lieutenant

Harimann Estate
,
Hightown
Quests
Repentance

Lord Harriman
(father)
Ruxton Harimann
(husband)
Flora Harimann
(daughter)
Brett Harimann
(son)
Appearances
Dragon Age II
-
The Exiled Prince
Lady
Johane Harimann
is the matriarch of the noble
Harimann family
of
Kirkwall
.
Background
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Lady Harimann was the mastermind behind the assassination of the
Vaels
, the ruling family of
Starkhaven
. Lady Johane took control of the Harimann family following her
father
's death. She murdered the Vaels (who had been long-time friends of the Harimanns until Johane's betrayal) in order to further her own family's power. She placed Goran Vael on the throne of Starkhaven, as she believed she could easily manipulate him. To solidify her hold, she prepared to force her daughter,
Flora
, into marriage with Goran.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Sebastian Vael
enlists the aid of
Hawke
in visiting the
Harimann Estate
after he discoveres that Lady Harimann was behind the murder of his parents and brothers. Inside the estate, the Harimanns are shown to be behaving very oddly, which Sebastian comments is completely out of character.
In the caves which run beneath the estate, Lady Harimann is discovered convening with a
Desire Demon
,
Allure
. It transpires that she unearthed the
Demon
while expanding the Estate and used her family, giving them to the desire demon in order to gain more power in an attempt to control Starkhaven. She naively believed that she was strong enough to resist the demon but it subtly influenced her until all she could think of was seizing Starkhaven. Lady Johane attacks Hawke and Sebastian but is killed and her family freed from the demon's clutches.
Quests
Repentance
Notes
Although Lady Harimann is a blood mage in gameplay, when asked whether her mother was a mage, Flora says that they've never had magic in their family and that this might have made her mother too confident when it came to dealing with demons
Wynne
mentions that mages can only be born, not made. A
non-mage Inquisitor
, even with
the anchor
fused to their hand never gets magical powers either, which is confirmed by
Solas
. Demons can bestow magical powers, but only once in full possession of a body and the only powers they can bestow are their own, based on their nature. This could indicate that Johane was an
apostate
her entire life and somehow managed to conceal it from everyone who knew her (including her own family and allies) for decades, all without anyone ever having any doubts or suspicions. Unless Johane was a completely unflappable little girl to the point of being almost emotionless (since magic answers to emotions during childhood), hiding her true nature for so long would have been all but impossible, especially in Kirkwall.

======================================================================

“I would rather die a mage than live as a templar puppet.”
Character
Karl Thekla
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Class
Mage
(
Tranquil
)
Affiliation
Circle of Magi
Location
Kirkwall Chantry
Quests
Tranquility
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Karl Thekla
is a
mage
friend and ex-lover of
Anders
who resides in
Kirkwall
.
Background
Karl spent many years at
Kinloch Hold
, the
Fereldan
Circle of Magi
. There, he befriended and eventually fell in love with
Anders
, another apprentice. They were inseparable for years; Anders never attempted to escape while he was with Karl. Shortly after passing his
Harrowing
, Karl was transferred to the
Gallows
, which required new talent. A few weeks later, Anders escaped Kinloch Hold to try and reunite with Karl in Kirkwall but was caught by templars on the docks in
West Hill
. Though they wouldn't see each other again for years, they continued to exchange letters.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Karl is involved in the quest
Tranquility
. Anders asks
Hawke
to assist him in helping Karl escape from the Circle. Anders has been corresponding with Karl for some time and has arranged to meet him in the
Kirkwall Chantry
. In reality, Karl was caught in contact with Anders and was made
Tranquil
at the behest of Ser
Otto Alrik
. When Anders and Hawke arrive at the Chantry to help Karl, they realize the
Templars
are using Karl to lure Anders into a trap.
When confronted by Karl, Anders becomes enraged and unleashes
Vengeance
. Vengeance's emergence brings with it a piece of
the Fade
, which, for a short time, restores Karl's emotions. Karl confesses that he does not want to live as an emotionless puppet serving the templars, and he begs Anders to end his life. Hawke can advise Anders to grant Karl his wish or ask Anders to spare Karl. Either way, Anders will kill Karl in order to put him out of his misery, apologizing for failing Karl before killing him.
If the player chooses to visit Anders in Act 1 after completing the quest, Anders, if Hawke is male, may admit that he and Karl were once lovers, and that Karl was his "first."
Quests
Tranquility
Quotes
"Anders. I know you too well. I knew you would never give up."
"I was too rebellious. Like you. The Templars knew I had to be… made an example of."
"Now! It's fading! [monotonous voice] Why do you look at me like that?"

Hawke can:
convince the mages to go with Karras and Thrask to the Circle.
lie to Karras that the apostates are dead and that Decimus has fled to the Wounded Coast through the caves. This requires either a sarcastic Hawke or having Varric in the party. Varric will also feed Karras a line that Hawke is either Ser Hawke from the Fereldan

kill Karras and the templars who came with him. Thrask will help Hawke.

in an attempt to avenge his death.

In Act 3, Hawke can talk to Karras in the Gallows courtyard. He tells Hawke that
Meredith
"has sent to
Val Royeaux
for the

," which grants
Codex entry: The Right of Annulment
.

Character

Jamie Glover
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Kelder Vanard
is a murderer hiding in a
Ruined Passage
outside of
Kirkwall
.
Background
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Kelder Vanard is the son of Magistrate
Vanard
and a serial killer who targets
elves
, particularly children. He claims to do so because demons in his head tell him to–something which the
Circle of Magi
has disputed–and because the young elves have "no right to be so beautiful." He says that his father attempted to stop him but failed to do so. He is sick of his own life and wants to die.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Kelder is involved in the quest
Magistrate's Orders
.
Magistrate
Vanard
asks Hawke to look for a dangerous criminal who escaped and is now hiding in a
Ruined Passage
beneath some
Abandoned Ruins
on the
Wounded Coast
. Vanard has already sent members of the
Kirkwall City Guard
there, but they were slaughtered by unspecified "creatures". Vanard promises
Hawke
future support in exchange for returning the criminal alive and unharmed.
At the ruins,
Elren
, an
elven
merchant from Kirkwall, tells Hawke that the criminal has kidnapped and killed his daughter,
Lia
, and asks that Hawke execute him. Lia is in fact still alive inside the ruins. She pleads with Hawke to spare Kelder's life, as she believes that
demons
made him hurt her.
When Hawke finally confronts the murderer, they learn that he is Magistrate Vanard's son. They can choose to return him to the magistrate, which will result in a 1
reward (2
with blackmail) and rivalry from their companions, or kill him. Killing him will result in a reward of 1
from
Elren
at the entrance, approval from some companions, and a promise of revenge from the magistrate.
Quests
Magistrate's Orders

Keran
is a
templar

Kirkwall
.
Background
Keran is one of many templar recruits being trained in
the Gallows
in 9:31
Dragon
, along with
Hugh
,
Paxley
,
Ruvena
and
Wilmod
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
During the quest
Enemies Among Us
,
Macha
asks
Hawke
to help her find her missing brother, Keran.
When speaking to the templar recruits in the Gallows, it is revealed that several other recruits have disappeared as well. Upon further investigation, it turns out that blood mages led by
Tarohne
have been kidnapping recruits that spent time at the
Blooming Rose
in order to turn them into
abominations
. Keran is the only surviving victim. If
Merrill
or
Anders
are present when Hawke rescues Keran, Hawke can ask them to verify if Keran is possessed. Both of them will state that he is safe.
Hawke can persuade
Cullen
either to allow Keran to stay with the Order, or to expel him. Hawke can also mention that they checked that Keran is not possessed without mentioning how exactly they did it via a special dialogue option.
If Keran was expelled from the Order, his father can be found in
Lowtown
near Gamlen's house, stumbling and drunk. Keran and Macha are standing not far away from him. The quest
A Debt in the Family
becomes available.
In any case, Hawke receives a
Letter from Macha
.
Alternatively, if Keran remained in the Templar Order then
Ser Roderick
will be
investigating
him at
The Hanged Man
.
Regardless of whether Keran stayed with or was dismissed from the Order, he takes part in a radical Templar-Mage group lead by
Thrask
which kidnaps Hawke's sibling or companion during the quest
Best Served Cold
. He claims to have been against the kidnapping, due to his own experience, and tells Hawke where to find them. He can then either be killed or reported to Meredith or released, in which case he intends to leave
Kirkwall
. If Keran is spared, he is later seen outside
the Hanged Man
, stating that he can't be a templar with Meredith in charge of the Order. In
Dragon Age Keep
there is an option in which Keran rejoins the templars under Knight-Captain Cullen's discretion and promise to keep a very close eye on the recruit, despite this seems to be not implemented in-game, the option is actually "Gave Keran to the templars", which is within the choices of what to do with Keran during the
Best Served Cold
questline. The description simply implying what happened "afterward".

"
Ketojan
" is the name given to the
Qunari
mage
placed into
Hawke
's care in
Dragon Age II

Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Ketojan is a
Saarebas
, a Qunari mage who shares the same name-title like
Sten
and the
Arishok
; showing his role as designated by the Qun.
Chantry
sister
Petrice
believes he wishes to escape the oppression of his people, and sends Hawke to escort him to the
Qun deserters
during the quest
Shepherding Wolves
. In truth, he wishes to live by the Qun, despite how he's leashed by his
Arvaarad
and the fact that he would have been killed anyway.
If Hawke is forced to fight the Arvaarad in order to allow Ketojan his chance at freedom, and if Anders is in the party after the fight, the following argument will occur:
Hawke
: "What if I hadn't killed Arvaarad? Could you have returned if I let these others live?"
Ketojan
: "No."
Hawke
: "You were doomed from the start?"
Ketojan
: "I was outside my karataam. I may be corrupted. I don't know. How I return is my choice."
Anders
: "Of all the ridiculous, spineless, mind-controlled, senseless piece of shit arguments I've ever heard!"
Ketojan
: "What comfort has freedom brought you, mage? You would have more if you submitted to the Qun."
Hawke can offer him to return to Petrice, but he says she wasn't honest and he's afraid of her templar guard. Hawke can also offer him to join the Tal-Vashoth, but he rejects this, because he doesn't want to abandon the Qun like them.
Regardless of Hawke's responses, Ketojan ultimately refuses to live without the Qun and its purpose and commits suicide by his fire magic. Before his demise he will gift Hawke an
amulet
.

“We've lost it all. Everything your father and I built.”
Character
Leandra Amell
Title
Lady

,

,

(mother)

(husband)

(brother)

Dragon Age II
Legacy

Heroes of Dragon Age
Dragon Age: Inquisition
(mentioned)
Leandra Amell
is the widow of apostate mage
Malcolm Hawke
, and the mother of
Hawke
,
Bethany
, and
Carver
. Her birth family, the
Amells
, are nobility in
Kirkwall
.
Background
Leandra was born in
Kirkwall
in the later years of the
Blessed Age
, the first child of the powerful Lord Aristide Amell and his wife Lady Bethann Walker. Her brother
Gamlen
was born a year later. Their parents favored Leandra and doted on her, showering her with gifts and attention. While Gamlen grew to resent their parents' favoritism, the siblings adored each other.
At age eleven, Leandra was betrothed to
Guillaume de Launcet
, the eldest son of Comte Reynaud de Launcet. They met the next summer at the comte's country estate.
In 9:05
Dragon
, Leandra and her family attended a banquet at Viscount
Perrin Threnhold
's estate in honor of the visiting Grand Duchess
Florianne de Chalons
. There, she met
Malcolm Hawke
, a member of Kirkwall's
Circle of Magi
. Gamlen helped them sneak out to the balcony to talk in private when he noticed the way his sister looked at Malcolm.
They left the estate deeply in love with one another.
Malcolm and Leandra continued to meet in secret over the next few months, with Gamlen's continued assistance. When Leandra realized she was pregnant, they decided to run away and wed in secret. By the time Malcolm managed to escape
the Gallows
and find a ship willing to offer them passage to
Ferelden
, Leandra's parents had discovered her pregnancy. Furious that his daughter had chosen a mage, Lord Aristide sent Templars in pursuit of Malcolm. While hiding-out in
Lowtown
, Malcolm was approached by
Warden-Commander
Larius
with an offer to assist the
Grey Wardens
in exchange for reuniting him with Leandra. Malcolm agreed to his conditions and prior to setting off for the
Vimmark Mountains
he sent Leandra a message telling her that they could finally be free once he returned.
This section contains spoilers for
:
Dragon Age II
.
The Wardens needed a non-tainted mage to perform a
blood magic
ritual to keep
Corypheus
contained. They threatened Leandra's life to get Malcolm to comply.
When Malcolm returned to Kirkwall with a
Grey Warden
escort, Lord Aristide told his daughter to choose between her family or Malcolm, saying that everything would be forgiven if she chose to renounce her apostate lover. Leandra chose Malcolm; Lord Aristide disowned her. Her mother refused to see Leandra before she left.
Malcolm and Leandra left for Ferelden that night. They settled in a small village near
Amaranthine
for a time, where Malcolm worked as a farmhand and Leandra as a seamstress. Their first child,
Hawke
, was born a few months later. They were forced to move often to avoid being captured by
templars
. Leandra's mother died of cholera around 9:10; Lord Aristide followed her a year later. As Leandra had recently given birth to twins,
Bethany
(named after Lady Bethann) and
Carver
, she was unable to attend the funeral.
This section contains spoilers for
:
Dragon Age II
.
Unbeknownst to her, her parents had come to forgive her. Lord Aristide left everything to Leandra, leaving Gamlen only a small stipend to be administered by her.
The Hawke family eventually settled down in
Lothering
in 9:20 Dragon. Malcolm died seven years later.
Appearance
Leandra's appearance varies with Hawke's facial preset and skintone
Leandra has one of several facial structures and hair styles, depending on the customization of the player's character. The selection works as follows:
There are three base facial shapes that each family member can have. Hawkes using the default Hawke appearance or any of the first three presets will get the first head shape, Hawkes using the second three presets will get the second head shape, and Hawkes using the final three presets (or any modded presets past that) will get the third shape.
Each of the three head shapes has three variations - one with a pale skintone, one with a medium skintone, and one with a dark skintone, and each with a different hairstyle. Which of these variations is used by the game depends on Hawke's skintone; the first four skintones will result in the light-skinned version of Leandra, the second four in the medium-skinned version, and the final four in the dark-skinned version. The same applies for
Carver
,
Bethany
and
Gamlen
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for
:
Dragon Age II
.
Shortly after the
Battle of Ostagar
, where at least one of her children had fought as a soldier in service to
King Cailan
, Leandra escapes
Lothering's destruction
with her family, the darkspawn vanguard in close pursuit. During their flight through the
Blightlands
, one of the twins is slain by an
ogre
. Stricken with grief, she blames Hawke for this, as she believes that they could have prevented her child from "charging off." Leandra and her remaining children, along with
Aveline Vallen
, escape to
Gwaren
with the aid of
Flemeth
, the
Witch of the Wilds
. There, they take a ship to
Kirkwall
, where Leandra's family, the
Amells
have an
estate
. However, Leandra's younger brother
Gamlen
lost the estate some years earlier due to his gambling habit. To help his family gain entrance into the city, Gamlen commits Leandra's children to working for either
mercenaries
or
smugglers
for a year, much to her dismay.
Leandra and Gamlen experience some conflict over money, as well as the loss of the Amell estate. Hawke and their sibling can
go to the vault
of the old estate to find their grandfather's will, which shows that their grandfather left the estate to Leandra and her children while Gamlen was to receive a stipend, controlled by her.
Leandra still expresses sadness at the loss of her child in Lothering, but does not seem to blame Hawke for the death anymore; indeed, if Hawke asks her about it directly, she apologizes for having lashed out in her grief.
Before Hawke sets out for the
Deep Roads expedition
, Leandra pleads for her other child to stay behind: she fears losing both children, should the expedition fail.
Upon Hawke's profitable return from the
Deep Roads
, the family regains control of the old Amell estate from the slavers and Leandra tells Hawke how proud she is. She talks about finding a suitable partner for Hawke and even entertains the idea of remarrying. If Hawke is in a
romance
, she briefly acknowledges it.
Bodahn Feddic
and his son
Sandal
become part of Hawke's household at this point; Bodahn refers to Leandra as "Mistress Amell" and appears to be quite fond of her.
Leandra walking towards Hawke
When Hawke investigates the
mystery
over the missing women in Kirkwall, Leandra is abducted by the white-lily serial killer while on her way to visit Gamlen. Following the killer's trail, Hawke finds that Leandra has been murdered and pieced together with parts of other women by the
killer
, kept alive by his magic as he believes Leandra's face resembles that of his deceased wife. During his battle with Hawke, the killer causes Leandra to appear in the possessed form of a
desire demon
along with his other victims, Ninette de Carrac and
Alessa
. Before Leandra dies, she tells Hawke how proud she is.
Years after Leandra's death, Hawke still finds it difficult to enter Leandra's room in the estate.
If Leandra is deceased during the events of
Legacy
, her ghost appears to Hawke at the end of the
DLC
. She converses with her child about her husband,
Malcolm
.
Varric
, in his role as narrator, admits that this conversation did not actually take place, but says that he feels Hawke deserves the closure and so he has added it to their story. The conversation will still happen if
Legacy
is completed before her death, but will have a slightly different tone (and of course will need no explanation from Varric).

Trivia
Leandra is related to the human
Warden
from the
Magi Origin
; she is the cousin of the Warden's mother, Revka.
As the daughter of nobility, Leandra was taught how to ride and shoot a bow, though her tutor described her archery skills as "fair to middling at best".
Leandra is a talented lute player, having mastered the intricate melodies of "The Red-Breasted Robin" at the age of eight. She also can recite the names of the great
Orlesian
houses and their histories from memory.

Background
Lord Harimann is the noble who convinced the
Viscount
of Kirkwall to send aid to
Denerim
during the
Fifth Blight
. For that reason, many nobles in the Free Marches resent him.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
While tiding up some
Loose Ends
given to
Hawke
by
Meeran
, the leader of the Red Iron mercenary company, Hawke's mission is to kill Lord Harimann and to rescue one of Meeran's men,
Gustav
.
During the conversation between Hawke and Harimann when they first meet, Hawke has the choice to kill the lord or to listen to him. If he chooses so, he learns that Harimann was the chief proponent behind sending help to Ferelden during the Blight. Hawke can then decide a course of action and report to Meeran after complying or disobeying.
If Harimann was spared, Hawke can convince Meeran that Harimann escaped, in which case Meeran will swear to kill him personally. Alternatively, Hawke can come clean, in which case Meeran will swear to kill Harimann himself, but also ambush Hawke at night in
Lowtown
.
Lord Harimann died at some point prior to 9:34
Dragon
, either because of Hawke or under unknown circumstances and leadership of the family passed to his daughter, Lady
Johane Harimann
.

Dragon Age II
Madam Lusine
is the proprietor of
the Blooming Rose
, a brothel located in the Red Lantern District in
Kirkwall
's
Hightown
.
Involvement
She can be found in the main room of the building, usually near the bar area. She tends to look down on
Fereldans
. Should
Hawke
first attempt to patronize her establishment during Act 1, she assumes them to be in extreme poverty, to a point of actually suspecting forgery should Hawke prove able to pay for the premium service. Upon inquiry, she offers you the services of the Blooming Rose, for a price: "Two sovereigns for premium service. One sovereign for standard service. Fifty silver and someone may touch you. Briefly." There are rumors that she gives a "special service" to loyal costumers.
Act 2: Spending several visits of "best service" leads to a special choice ("Blow my mind") which leads to a comical scene of literary reading.
Act 3: Spending several visits of "best service" leads to a special choice ("Something exotic") which leads to a unique encounter.

Background

's sources say that a woman by the name of Macha has been desperately seeking a particular
templar
. She's been spotted outside of the
Chantry
in
Hightown
during the day.

This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Macha is involved in the quest

.
She is very worried about her templar brother,
Keran
. He used to write to her every day when suddenly the letters stopped arriving. She asks
Hawke
to speak with the templar recruits in the
Gallows
to find out what happened to him.

as

PAGE: Malcolm Hawke
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Malcolm_Hawke
======================================================================

“My magic will serve that which is best in me, not that which is most base.”
Character
Malcolm Hawke
Title
Junior enchanter
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Class
Mage
Specialization
Blood Mage
Affiliation
Circle of Magi
(formerly)
Family
Aristide Amell
(father-in-law)
Bethann Walker
(mother-in-law)
Leandra Amell
(wife)
Hawke
(son/daughter)
Bethany Hawke
(daughter)
Carver Hawke
(son)
Gamlen Amell
(brother-in-law)
Charade Amell
(niece)
Voice
Nicholas Boulton
Appearances
Dragon Age II
(mentioned)
Legacy
(ghost)
Dragon Age: The Veilguard
(mentioned)
Malcolm Hawke
was the father of
Hawke
,
Bethany
and
Carver
, as well as the husband of
Leandra
. He was an
apostate
mage. He died in 9:27 Dragon, three years before the outbreak of the
Fifth Blight
which forced his wife and children to flee to
Kirkwall
.
Background
Malcolm Hawke was born in
Ferelden
. He was brought to
Kirkwall's Circle
late in the
Blessed Age
as a young apprentice. He was shown to be an adept mage and was learning complex spells by the age of fourteen until his advancements slowed to the level of his fellow apprentices.
Senior Enchanter Consuelon
believed he was concealing his talents in order to not draw attention to himself while in the Gallows. He undertook his
Harrowing
at the age of nineteen.
In 9:05 Dragon, he met
Leandra Amell
while the Circle mages performed at Viscount
Perrin Threnhold
's banquet held for
Grand Duchess Florianne
. With the help of Leandra's brother,
Gamlen
, Malcolm and Leandra met more privately on a side balcony.
Malcolm and Leandra continued to meet over the following months. With the aid of the Templar Ser Maurevar Carver, Malcolm was able to sneak out of the Gallows to meet with Leandra. When Leandra became pregnant with his child, Malcolm asked her to run away with him. She agreed, and they married in secret. Templar records reveal that Ser Maurevar assisted Malcolm in escaping the Circle, though it is unclear if he was an accomplice in the theft of Malcolm's
phylactery
.
By the time Malcolm secured passage—for himself and Leandra—to Ferelden via Kirkwall's docks, Lord Aristide Amell had learned that his daughter was pregnant with the mage's child. Lord Aristide forbade Leandra to leave the family home and sent men after Malcolm. Leandra was able to get a message to Malcolm, via Gamlen, warning him of the danger he was in.
Hunted and nearly penniless, Malcolm was faced with a difficult dilemma: leave on the ship without Leandra or stay and face the wrath of Lord Aristide and the templars. Refusing to leave Leandra behind in Kirkwall, Malcolm went into hiding in a
Lowtown
tavern where he was approached by
Warden-Commander
Larius
. Larius demanded a service of Malcolm and in return, the
Grey Wardens
would help in reuniting him with Leandra. Malcolm agreed.
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Malcolm briefly worked with the
Grey Wardens
when they required a non-Warden mage to renew the weakening seals of the secret prison under the
Vimmark Mountains
near Kirkwall, where the ancient Darkspawn
Corypheus
had been bound. They chose Malcolm Hawke and forced him to use
blood magic
to strengthen the seals binding Corypheus and
several other demons
. As a result, the seals could only be broken using the blood of Malcolm's children, making them a
target
for those trying to free Corypheus. Warden-Commander
Larius
secured Malcolm's cooperation by threatening to murder Leandra, at the time pregnant with Hawke. Malcolm agreed to his terms but also stipulated that, along with Leandra's safety, Larius also paid him for his services and convinced Lord Aristide Amell to allow Leandra and him to leave Kirkwall with impunity.
After Malcolm provided his service to the Wardens, Malcolm arrived at the Amell family estate with a contingent of Grey Wardens, and he demanded that Leandra be brought to him. Leandra came out alone, and she told him that she was free to leave. That night they boarded a ship to Ferelden. After that, they were constantly moving to avoid being captured by the
Templars
. At the same time, the Grey Wardens were also monitoring Malcolm and his family, but lost track of him in 9:17 Dragon.
Much to Malcolm's dismay, as he did not want his children to be ostracized for their magic, his daughter Bethany (and potentially Hawke) inherited his powers. He taught them how to correctly use their powers and how to keep them a secret. As a result, he spent comparatively little time with his youngest non-mage child, Carver.
In 9:20 Dragon, he and his family settled down on the outskirts of
Lothering
, where he made every effort to ensure that his children didn't fear magic, and were well insulated against those who did.
He died seven years later, in 9:27 Dragon, leaving the welfare of his family up to his wife and his eldest child.

Notes
Bethany tells Merrill her father died during the Blight, not 3 years before.
While
Codex entry: The Fugitive's Mantle
and
Codex entry: Malcolm's Bequest
state that Malcolm was an apostate who worked as a mercenary when he met Leandra; Leandra, Gamlen and
Dragon Age: The World of Thedas Volume 2
state that he was a Circle mage in Kirkwall.
Trivia
Bethany tells
Anders
that he reminds her of Malcolm.
Hawke is able to inherit Malcolm's raiments through the
Mage Item Pack
DLC
for
Dragon Age II
.
It is suggested that Malcolm and Hawke share the same personality (Diplomatic/Humorous/Aggressive) in a conversation with Anders during
Mark of the Assassin
, and again with Leandra in the conclusion of
Legacy
.
Nicholas Boulton provides the voice for both Male Hawke and Malcolm.
Ser Maurevar Carver once said the reason he let Malcolm escape the Circle of Magi was that "Rule does not serve by caging the best of us."

======================================================================
PAGE: Mara Hartling
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Mara_Hartling
======================================================================

Character
Mara Hartling
Race
Human
Gender
Female
Affiliation
Amell family
Reinhardt family
Family
Charade Amell
(daughter)
Appearances
Dragon Age II
(mentioned)
Mara Hartling
is the mother of
Charade Amell
. She died in 9:36
Dragon
.
Background
Mara's family, the Hartlings, used to be noteworthy traders, with trade routes between
Nevarra
and the
Free Marches
. By Mara's time, their standing had diminished considerably. Mara's mother was the
Amell family
's old head cook, while she worked as a chambermaid at the
Amell Family estate
.
Mara was befriended and eventually fell in love with
Gamlen Amell
, in charge of the estate at the time. Gamlen and Mara both nursed Lord Aristide and Lady Bethann after they fell sick with cholera, but although they got better, they never regained their full strength. Lady Bethann died after a second bout in 9:10, while Lord Aristide died one year later in 9:11.
Despite the numerous scandals faced by the Amells, Mara stayed with Gamlen. She eventually found employment with the Reinhardt family.
Eventually Mara left Gamlen when he continued to spend his nights gambling, saying that she wouldn't let him waste another life like he'd wasted his.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for
:
Dragon Age II
.
During the quest
Gamlen's Greatest Treasure
, it is revealed that Mara left Gamlen because he had been too obsessed with finding the
Gem of Keroshek
, and that she was pregnant with Gamlen's daughter Charade at the time. Mara did not tell Gamlen she was pregnant when she left him, and he therefore had no idea about the existence of his daughter. Mara repeatedly told Charade she was "so much like [her father]", but never revealed Gamlen's identity to Charade until she was on her deathbed.
She died in 9:36 Dragon, a year before the events of Act 3 in
Dragon Age II
.
Trivia
Unlike the rest of
Hawke
's family members, Mara's daughter's appearance is fixed and does not change to match Hawke's appearance at creation. This apparent discrepancy is explained when Gamlen "thanks the Maker" that Charade got her mother's looks. Mara is described as having bright blue eyes and a thick mane of chestnut hair.
References

PAGE: Maraas
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age II characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Maraas
======================================================================

Character
Maraas
Title
Mercenary
Race
Qunari
Gender
Male
Class
Warrior
Affiliation
Tal-Vashoth
Location
Wounded Coast
Tal-Vashoth Cavern
,
Kirkwall
Hanged Man
,
Kirkwall

Voice
Keith Szarabajka
Appearances
Dragon Age II
Maraas
is a
Tal-Vashoth
former bandit now working as a mercenary.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Maraas is a
Qunari
warrior, first encountered on the
Wounded Coast
during the quest
Blackpowder Promise
.
The Champion
can convince him to turn against the other renegade Qunari using the specialised
aggressive dialogue option open to
an aggressive Hawke
.
This will not be his first time deserting his people, however, the first time being from the
Qun
, where he didn't accept the role he was given. After leaving the Qun, he joined a band of
Tal-Vashoth
residing in a
cavern
outside
Kirkwall
. In time however he left the Tal-Vashoth and even encourages Hawke to kill them. Hawke can try to hire him, however Maraas will decline, payment or not, as he does not wish to murder for money. However, if Hawke has made mostly aggressive choices, it is possible through dialogue to convince Maraas to fight with Hawke against the Tal-Vashoth. Hawke can tell him that the last man standing decides what is right, and Maraas will agree to help kill the Tal-Vashoth and their leader.
He later takes up residence in the
Hanged Man
during Act 3. Having taken the name Maraas as his own, he works as a mercenary, but will not work for the Champion, because he prefers simple jobs over ones from people with status, as he dislikes fighting for a cause. He explains that he has picked his own name, since he does not have any role in the Qun and Qunari are named after their place in society. He also reveals that after
First Battle of Kirkwall
the remaining Qunari and Tal-Vashoth in the surrounding regions were eliminated just in case.
Quests
Blackpowder Promise
Trivia
His self-given name means "nothing" in the
Qunari language
.
His name is an anagram of
Armaas
, another notable
Tal-Vashoth
.
Bugs

Tal-Vashoth
(dialogue option available only to an aggressive Hawke during the quest

on the
Wounded Coast
) even if that was not the case. This remains the same regardless of whether or not you chose such options during your dialogue with him.

Marlein Selbrech
is a minor noble in the city of
